So in the itinerary in Changchun these days, most of them have seven commercial vehicles with heated seats. Special thanks to the front office manager Li Yufei, the front desk service Ma Shibin and the driver are all off work, but they acted as drivers temporarily to pick me up at night Brother Yan Kun, the person on duty.

The room environment is very clean, the details are true, equipped with an air purifier, the room is very warm, as if there is geothermal heat, a little dry. There are a lot of literary works on the bookshelf, and the auntie in the guest room also helped me fold the clothes, wash the socks, and sent fruits and homemade snacks in the hotel. Everything is not so gorgeous, but everything is very down-to-earth and warm, making you feel It's like going to a relative's house, someone takes care of your daily necessities.

The breakfast is also very rich, including xylitol yogurt, Northeastern special stews, and the pasta made by the hotel itself. They are all delicious. It can be seen that they are prepared with care.

The hotel is also equipped with a bath center and a fitness center. The fitness equipment is very complete. Although it is not particularly new, it is very useful. There is no damage or disrepair. The bath center has no time to go this time. It is really complete and one-stop service. Try to meet all your needs in the hotel.

In fact, I have stayed in some high-priced old-fashioned five-star hotels in the city center before, but it is really not as good as Herun's considerate service and care, which is even rare in the entire Northeast. The above list is only a part of the service staff whose names have been recorded. I really want to express my respect and thanks to the service team of Herun. I will definitely visit again next time. I wish everyone in the hotel better and better!
